Before departure, I compared many hotels and finally chose Kaiyuan Caribbean with hesitation because I saw some bad reviews. This is a hotel with its own playground and hot springs. They arranged us in a small villa opposite the lobby. It is also very convenient to have breakfast when traveling. The hotel staff also enthusiastically helped with the luggage and led the way. The room is very large, the bed is very comfortable, and there is a super large balcony with a green view. There are fruits and drinks every day, as well as snacks. The toiletries are also better, with children's toothbrushes and slippers. The only drawback is that there are no sanitary towels on the washbasin, only on the bedside table. In addition, I forgot to take a small bag when I left, and the hotel also sent it to me very quickly by SF Express. The only drawback is that there are no amusement facilities in the hotel. name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Boutique Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:3 Reviews
rating:3.7
posted:Posted April 8, 2024
msg:1. Arrival and reception:
- Arrival experience: The hotel is a bit remote, and there are construction sites around, which is a bit noisy. The hotel parking space is seriously insufficient. When there are many people, you need to park in the open space outside the hotel, which is a bit inconvenient. However, the housekeeper will take the initiative to add WeChat to communicate the day before, which is very good. During the stay, I asked the housekeeper questions and he responded very promptly, which is a good comment.
- Front desk reception: I arrived at about 12 o'clock, and they said there were no vacancies and asked me to wait for notification. As a result, it was more than 3 o'clock in the afternoon. I took the initiative to ask the housekeeper and found out that there were vacancies. The experience was average. The hotel's shuttle bus experience was good, and you can quickly call a car wherever you want to go.
2. Room:
- Room hygiene: The room hygiene is good, and it meets expectations overall
- Facility completeness: All the facilities are available, and there are benches and toiletries prepared for children, which is very good
- Comfort: The room is not very big, but it is enough for a family. But the pillow is a bit high, and my neck hurts when I sleep at night
3. Dining service:
- Restaurant environment: The restaurant is on the first floor and has a good location. But maybe because there were many people on holiday, breakfast was really crowded. You had to wait for a seat, and after you got a seat, you had to wait for someone to come and clean up. The overall waiting time for dining was a bit long.
- Food quality: There are quite a lot of food varieties, especially Chinese stir-fried dishes, which I personally like. But the experience on the second day was not very good, because there was no prompt at the place where you could get ice cream, and then I saw someone getting it. After I went over and got it, a waiter came over and said that ice cream was charged, 10 yuan per ball. This is the first time I have ever encountered a buffet breakfast with extra charges for ice cream in so many hotels. And the first few people obviously didn't spend money, and the waiter didn't care, but when it came to me, they started charging, which was really speechless.
4. Location and surroundings:
- Location: I basically came here for the amusement park and hot springs. The hotel package includes tickets, but it should be noted that it only includes tickets for 2 adults. If the child is over 1.1m, you have to pay extra tickets. There are no other recreational projects around. If you come in summer, there may be fruit picking, but it's a pity that I went too early this time. I went to the hot springs. There are only 10 pools in total. There were too few people that day, so only 4 pools were opened. The overall experience was average. If you come just for the hot springs, I don't recommend it. It's not cost-effective.
- Transportation convenience: It's quite convenient to drive by yourself, but it may not be very convenient if you don't have a car
5. Overall evaluation:
- The hotel room is clean and comfortable, and the housekeeper responds promptly. It's just that the service in the restaurant is a bit inferior. If you come to the amusement park, it's a good choice to stay here for one or two nights.
- Recommendation index: recommended

msg:The newly opened hotel, the two-night package coupon I grabbed before is very cost-effective. Taking advantage of the fact that there are few people now, I take my baby out for a walk. I have work during the day on Friday. When I leave in the afternoon, I arrive at the hotel and it is close to the meal time. The service staff in the lobby are very enthusiastic , I also upgraded the villa room for me, the area is very large and the mattress is very comfortable. Another major feature of the hotel is the 1V1 butler service. In particular, our butler, Mrs. Yang (Yang Tao), is too enthusiastic. She gave us a rafting ticket, absolutely 100 points! On the day of check-in, I had dinner at the Chinese restaurant and ordered a set meal for 2-3 people. When it came up, the amount was too much and the taste was very good. The environment of the hotel is quite quiet. There are still many places under construction. There will be cute pet hotels and hot springs next year. I will consider coming again next time I come to Anji!

msg:The butler service is good. I use 799 Ctrip room coupons, so Kaiyuan Platinum does not have any courtesy, and catering can only get 5% off. The Chinese restaurant is a catering system (the hotel is only a franchised Kaiyuan). However, the house coupons that Sen Bo bought before had all the benefits except the room upgrade. In fact, the park is not very interesting to play. For the same price, Senbo is recommended. I booked a Chinese restaurant for my baby's birthday. In fact, the dishes served by Marriott at the same price are better, but this place is more convenient, so I reluctantly chose this place. Generally speaking, the hotel facilities are relatively new, there are bathtubs, and the breakfast is OK. But there is no particularly prominent part. I personally think that the park is not worth visiting.
